I would not recommend anyone coming here for urgent care.

I came here to get my stitches removed. I made an appointment and showed up on time. There was nobody at the front desk when I arrived. I waited 45 minutes before the doctor saw me. The doctor was friendly, and seemed to have done a good job.

However, about two weeks later I found a small piece of stitch (~‚Öõ in.) still remaining beneath my newly closed wound. I returned to the place and asked the doctor to remove it. I couldn't believe when he said he couldn't see the remaining stitch. I had three people looking at it before I went back to the center, and they all saw it clearly. The doctor kept stressing that I was concerned due to cosmetic reason, when I never said a word about the potential scar. He said he could cut my wound open again, or I could wait for it to come out itself (medically speaking, this is a rare possibility). Such an unprofessional and irresponsible doctor he was! I visited this office back in March of 2019 when I had a case of swimmer‚Äôs ear. I could easily say this visit was one of the most uncomfortable and unsatisfying visits I have ever had in my entire life; if I could give 0 stars I would be more than happy to give 0 stars.

I also felt very rushed out of the room as well; Dr. Zhong clearly showed a lack of genuine concern for his patients and gave off an ‚Äúok, next patient‚Äù attitude.

I only received a verbal consultation, and I used Dr. Zhong‚Äôs prescription for a week with absolutely no result; my right ear was still completely clogged and had a muffled sound. < Review>
The guy that helped me with an acoustic and an electric setup was friendly. Both guitars are in much better shape.

My fender hellcat acoustic had action that was way too high. It's much easier to play after he lowered the bridge, strung up some new strings and adjusted the truss rod. Sustain is improved on higher frets as well since it's way easier to push down the strings. Super happy with this setup.

My Ibanez gio seemed impossible to intonate the g string when I left it and the action was set high to compensate for the last 4 frets not ringing out at all. He straightened out the truss rod, replaced the strings and lowered the action. Sustain is improved across the whole fretboard and the intonation seems to be fixed. There's still slight buzzing when I play hard, but it's a cheap electric and I wasn't expecting there not to be. Probably needs a little fretwork. For $50 bucks the other fixes made it worthwhile.

I'm happy with both setups. Best $110 I ever spent.<//Review>
